[30;1m975 | [0m[35m        #    traceback, even if it is obvious top cocotb maintainers.[0m
[30;1m976 | [0m[35m        #  - Using `NullTrigger` here instead of `result = completed[0].get()`[0m
[30;1m977 | [0m[35m        #    means we avoid inserting an `outcome.get` frame in the traceback[0m
[30;1m978 | [0m[35m        first_trigger = NullTrigger(_outcome=completed[0])[0m
